## Instruction

Please help me check which products are in my shop, filter out those that have been in stock for more than 90 days and have sold fewer than 10 units in the past 30 days. Move them to a product category named "Outlet/Clearance" ("/" is part of the name). Also, send an email to each of the subscribed customers.

You can find the email template under the workspace (please sort the products by stock-in time from earliest to latest; if the stock-in time is the same, then sort by discount ratio from small to large). The subscriber information is in subscriber.json.

### Local Workspace

```python

import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

# Load the product data from the saved file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/KY2YnUKUsxNqbALMbcGdTF.json', 'r') as f:
    products_data = json.load(f)

# Parse the products from the API response
products = json.loads(products_data)

# Calculate the date 90 days ago
ninety_days_ago = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=90)

# Filter products based on criteria:
# 1. In stock for more than 90 days (date_created < 90 days ago)
# 2. Sold fewer than 10 units in the past 30 days (sales_last_30_days < 10)

filtered_products = []

for product in products:
    # Parse the date_created
    date_created = datetime.fromisoformat(product['date_created_gmt'].replace('Z', '+00:00'))
    
    # Check if in stock for more than 90 days
    if date_created < ninety_days_ago:
        # Check sales_last_30_days in meta_data
        sales_last_30_days = None
        for meta in product.get('meta_data', []):
            if meta['key'] == 'sales_last_30_days':
                sales_last_30_days = int(meta['value'])
                break
        
        # If sales_last_30_days < 10 (or not found, assume 0)
        if sales_last_30_days is not None and sales_last_30_days < 10:
            filtered_products.append({
                'id': product['id'],
                'name': product['name'],
                'date_created': product['date_created'],
                'sales_last_30_days': sales_last_30_days,
                'regular_price': product['regular_price'],
                'sale_price': product['sale_price']
            })

# Sort by stock-in time (earliest to latest), then by discount ratio (small to large)
def calculate_discount_ratio(product):
    regular_price = float(product['regular_price']) if product['regular_price'] else 0
    sale_price = float(product['sale_price']) if product['sale_price'] else regular_price
    
    if regular_price > 0 and sale_price < regular_price:
        return (regular_price - sale_price) / regular_price
    return 0

filtered_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['date_created'], calculate_discount_ratio(x)))

print(f"Total products: {len(products)}")
print(f"Filtered products (in stock > 90 days, sales < 10): {len(filtered_products)}")
print("\nFiltered products:")
for p in filtered_products[:10]:  # Show first 10
    print(f"  - ID: {p['id']}, Name: {p['name']}, Created: {p['date_created']}, Sales: {p['sales_last_30_days']}")

# Save filtered products for later use
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/filtered_products.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(filtered_products, f, indent=2)

print(f"\nFiltered products saved to filtered_products.json")
 code
```

```python

import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

# Load the product data from the saved file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/KY2YnUKUsxNqbALMbcGdTF.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

# The data is already a dict with 'output' key containing the text
output_text = data['output']['text']
products = json.loads(output_text)

# Calculate the date 90 days ago
ninety_days_ago = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=90)

# Filter products based on criteria:
# 1. In stock for more than 90 days (date_created < 90 days ago)
# 2. Sold fewer than 10 units in the past 30 days (sales_last_30_days < 10)

filtered_products = []

for product in products:
    # Parse the date_created (removing timezone info for comparison)
    date_created_str = product['date_created_gmt'].replace('Z', '')
    date_created = datetime.fromisoformat(date_created_str)
    
    # Check if in stock for more than 90 days
    if date_created < ninety_days_ago:
        # Check sales_last_30_days in meta_data
        sales_last_30_days = None
        for meta in product.get('meta_data', []):
            if meta['key'] == 'sales_last_30_days':
                sales_last_30_days = int(meta['value'])
                break
        
        # If sales_last_30_days < 10 (or not found, assume 0)
        if sales_last_30_days is not None and sales_last_30_days < 10:
            filtered_products.append({
                'id': product['id'],
                'name': product['name'],
                'date_created': product['date_created'],
                'sales_last_30_days': sales_last_30_days,
                'regular_price': product['regular_price'],
                'sale_price': product['sale_price']
            })

# Sort by stock-in time (earliest to latest), then by discount ratio (small to large)
def calculate_discount_ratio(product):
    regular_price = float(product['regular_price']) if product['regular_price'] else 0
    sale_price = float(product['sale_price']) if product['sale_price'] else regular_price
    
    if regular_price > 0 and sale_price < regular_price:
        return (regular_price - sale_price) / regular_price
    return 0

filtered_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['date_created'], calculate_discount_ratio(x)))

print(f"Total products: {len(products)}")
print(f"Filtered products (in stock > 90 days, sales < 10): {len(filtered_products)}")
print("\nFiltered products (sorted by date, then discount ratio):")
for p in filtered_products[:20]:  # Show first 20
    discount = calculate_discount_ratio(p)
    print(f"  - ID: {p['id']}, Name: {p['name']}, Created: {p['date_created']}, Sales: {p['sales_last_30_days']}, Discount: {discount:.2%}")

# Save filtered products for later use
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/filtered_products.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(filtered_products, f, indent=2)

print(f"Filtered products saved to filtered_products.json")

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

# Load the product data from the saved file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/KY2YnUKUsxNqbALMbcGdTF.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

# The data has 'text' key containing the JSON string
output_text = data['text']
products = json.loads(output_text)

# Calculate the date 90 days ago
ninety_days_ago = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=90)

# Filter products based on criteria:
# 1. In stock for more than 90 days (date_created < 90 days ago)
# 2. Sold fewer than 10 units in the past 30 days (sales_last_30_days < 10)

filtered_products = []

for product in products:
    # Parse the date_created (removing timezone info for comparison)
    date_created_str = product['date_created_gmt'].replace('Z', '')
    date_created = datetime.fromisoformat(date_created_str)
    
    # Check if in stock for more than 90 days
    if date_created < ninety_days_ago:
        # Check sales_last_30_days in meta_data
        sales_last_30_days = None
        for meta in product.get('meta_data', []):
            if meta['key'] == 'sales_last_30_days':
                sales_last_30_days = int(meta['value'])
                break
        
        # If sales_last_30_days < 10 (or not found, assume 0)
        if sales_last_30_days is not None and sales_last_30_days < 10:
            filtered_products.append({
                'id': product['id'],
                'name': product['name'],
                'date_created': product['date_created'],
                'sales_last_30_days': sales_last_30_days,
                'regular_price': product['regular_price'],
                'sale_price': product['sale_price']
            })

# Sort by stock-in time (earliest to latest), then by discount ratio (small to large)
def calculate_discount_ratio(product):
    regular_price = float(product['regular_price']) if product['regular_price'] else 0
    sale_price = float(product['sale_price']) if product['sale_price'] else regular_price
    
    if regular_price > 0 and sale_price < regular_price:
        return (regular_price - sale_price) / regular_price
    return 0

filtered_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['date_created'], calculate_discount_ratio(x)))

print(f"Total products: {len(products)}")
print(f"Filtered products (in stock > 90 days, sales < 10): {len(filtered_products)}")
print("\nFiltered products (sorted by date, then discount ratio):")
for i, p in enumerate(filtered_products[:20]):  # Show first 20
    discount = calculate_discount_ratio(p)
    print(f"{i+1}. ID: {p['id']}, Name: {p['name']}, Created: {p['date_created']}, Sales: {p['sales_last_30_days']}, Discount: {discount:.2%}")

# Save filtered products for later use
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/filtered_products.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(filtered_products, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n‚úì Total filtered products: {len(filtered_products)}")
print(f"‚úì Filtered products saved to filtered_products.json")
 code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

# This script will process the task step by step
# Since we have 398 products across 4 pages, we need to analyze all of them

import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from pathlib import Path

# Load all product data from the saved files
product_files = [
    '/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/KY2YnUKUsxNqbALMbcGdTF.json',  # Page 1
    '/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/ejZX8h7x2ycwckpnsFyhun.json',  # Page 2
    '/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/B4FxpqHC8xam2jMzZCUPNi.json',  # Page 3
    '/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/KGavvbLvdHaKpg8ztN2BTD.json',  # Page 4
]

all_products = []
for file_path in product_files:
    try:
        with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
            data = json.load(f)
            products_json = json.loads(data['text'])
            all_products.extend(products_json)
            print(f"Loaded {len(products_json)} products from {Path(file_path).name}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error loading {file_path}: {e}")

print(f"\nTotal products loaded: {len(all_products)}")

# Calculate the date 90 days ago
ninety_days_ago = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=90)
print(f"90 days ago date: {ninety_days_ago.date()}")

# Filter products based on criteria
filtered_products = []

for product in all_products:
    # Parse the date_created
    date_created_str = product['date_created_gmt'].replace('T', ' ').replace('Z', '')
    date_created = datetime.fromisoformat(date_created_str)
    
    # Check if in stock for more than 90 days
    if date_created < ninety_days_ago:
        # Check sales_last_30_days in meta_data
        sales_last_30_days = None
        for meta in product.get('meta_data', []):
            if meta['key'] == 'sales_last_30_days':
                sales_last_30_days = int(meta['value'])
                break
        
        # If sales_last_30_days < 10
        if sales_last_30_days is not None and sales_last_30_days < 10:
            # Calculate discount ratio
            regular_price = float(product['regular_price']) if product['regular_price'] else 0
            sale_price = float(product['sale_price']) if product['sale_price'] else 0
            
            discount_ratio = 0
            if regular_price > 0 and sale_price > 0 and sale_price < regular_price:
                discount_ratio = (regular_price - sale_price) / regular_price
            
            filtered_products.append({
                'id': product['id'],
                'name': product['name'],
                'date_created': product['date_created'],
                'sales_last_30_days': sales_last_30_days,
                'regular_price': regular_price,
                'sale_price': sale_price,
                'discount_ratio': discount_ratio
            })

# Sort by stock-in time (earliest to latest), then by discount ratio (small to large)
filtered_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['date_created'], x['discount_ratio']))

print(f"\nFiltered products (in stock > 90 days, sales < 10): {len(filtered_products)}")
print("\nFirst 10 products:")
for i, p in enumerate(filtered_products[:10]):
    print(f"{i+1}. ID: {p['id']}, Name: {p['name']}, Created: {p['date_created']}, Sales: {p['sales_last_30_days']}, Discount: {p['discount_ratio']:.2%}")

# Save filtered products for later use
output_file = '/workspace/dumps/workspace/filtered_products.json'
with open(output_file, 'w') as f:
    json.dump(filtered_products, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n‚úì Filtered products saved to {output_file}")
print(f"‚úì Total products to move to Outlet/Clearance: {len(filtered_products)}")
 code
```

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import json

# I'll create a processing script that will work with the data
# Let's manually process a sample from the visible product data

# Sample products from the first page (from the earlier API call)
# I'll extract key information to demonstrate the filtering logic

sample_products_text = """
Product ID: 153, Name: Samsung Laptop v44, Created: 2025-10-07T23:07:26, Sales: 65
Product ID: 214, Name: AOC Laptop v198, Created: 2025-10-07T23:07:26, Sales: 184
Product ID: 306, Name: Sony Tablet v169, Created: 2025-10-07T23:07:26, Sales: 80
"""

# Calculate 90 days ago from now (assuming current date is around Oct 17, 2025 based on product dates)
current_date = datetime(2025, 10, 17)
ninety_days_ago = current_date - timedelta(days=90)

print(f"Current date (estimated): {current_date.date()}")
print(f"90 days ago: {ninety_days_ago.date()}")
print(f"Products created before {ninety_days_ago.date()} are candidates")

# Based on the product dates I saw:
# - Most recent products are from Oct 7, 2025
# - Older products go back to around May-June 2025
# - 90 days ago from Oct 17 would be July 19, 2025

# So products created before July 19, 2025 with sales < 10 in last 30 days qualify

print("\nProducts need to meet BOTH criteria:")
print("1. Created before July 19, 2025 (more than 90 days ago)")
print("2. Sales in last 30 days < 10")

print("\nFrom the sample data, products created in July 2025 or earlier with sales < 10 will qualify")
print("I need to process all 398 products to find matches...")

    f.write("Category 'Outlet/Clearance' created with ID: 16\n")
    f.write(f"Filter criteria: Created before {ninety_days_ago.date()}, Sales < 10\n")
    f.write("Status: Ready to process products\n")

print("\n‚úì Status file created")

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

# Create a comprehensive processing script
# This will generate the list of product IDs that need to be updated

processing_script = '''
# WooCommerce Product Processing Script
# This script processes products and identifies those needing category update

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import json

def process_products(products_json_text):
    """Process products from API JSON response"""
    products = json.loads(products_json_text)
    
    # Calculate 90 days ago
    current_date = datetime(2025, 10, 17)  # Estimated current date
    ninety_days_ago = current_date - timedelta(days=90)
    
    filtered = []
    
    for product in products:
        # Parse creation date
        date_str = product['date_created_gmt'].replace('T', ' ').replace('Z', '')
        date_created = datetime.fromisoformat(date_str)
        
        # Check if older than 90 days
        if date_created < ninety_days_ago:
            # Find sales_last_30_days in metadata
            sales = None
            for meta in product.get('meta_data', []):
                if meta['key'] == 'sales_last_30_days':
                    sales = int(meta['value'])
                    break
            
            # Check if sales < 10
            if sales is not None and sales < 10:
                regular_price = float(product.get('regular_price', 0) or 0)
                sale_price = float(product.get('sale_price', 0) or 0)
                
                discount_ratio = 0
                if regular_price > 0 and sale_price > 0:
                    discount_ratio = (regular_price - sale_price) / regular_price
                
                filtered.append({
                    'id': product['id'],
                    'name': product['name'],
                    'date_created': product['date_created'],
                    'sales': sales,
                    'regular_price': regular_price,
                    'sale_price': sale_price,
                    'discount_ratio': discount_ratio
                })
    
    return filtered

# This function will be used to process API responses
'''

# Save the script
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/process_products.py', 'w') as f:
    f.write(processing_script)

print("‚úì Processing script created: process_products.py")
print("\nNow I need to manually process the products from the API calls...")
print("Since the saved files have issues, I'll need to work with fresh API data")
 code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

# Read the latest API response (oldest products, sorted ascending)
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/G5y9WNkkBeMcGLmNjAjrWW.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)
    products = json.loads(data['text'])

# Filter criteria
cutoff_date = datetime(2025, 7, 19)  # 90 days before Oct 17, 2025

qualifying_products = []

for product in products:
    # Parse creation date
    date_str = product['date_created_gmt'].replace('T', ' ').replace('Z', '')
    date_created = datetime.fromisoformat(date_str)
    
    # Check if older than 90 days
    if date_created < cutoff_date:
        # Find sales_last_30_days
        sales = None
        for meta in product.get('meta_data', []):
            if meta['key'] == 'sales_last_30_days':
                sales = int(meta['value'])
                break
        
        # Check if sales < 10
        if sales is not None and sales < 10:
            regular_price = float(product.get('regular_price', 0) or 0)
            sale_price = float(product.get('sale_price', 0) or 0)
            
            discount_ratio = 0
            if regular_price > 0 and sale_price > 0:
                discount_ratio = (regular_price - sale_price) / regular_price
            
            qualifying_products.append({
                'id': product['id'],
                'name': product['name'],
                'date_created': product['date_created'],
                'sales': sales,
                'regular_price': regular_price,
                'sale_price': sale_price if sale_price > 0 else regular_price,
                'discount_ratio': discount_ratio
            })

# Sort by date (earliest first), then by discount ratio (smallest first)
qualifying_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['date_created'], x['discount_ratio']))

print(f"Found {len(qualifying_products)} qualifying products from this batch:")
for i, p in enumerate(qualifying_products, 1):
    print(f"{i}. ID:{p['id']:4} {p['name']:30} Created:{p['date_created'][:10]} Sales:{p['sales']:2} Discount:{p['discount_ratio']:.1%}")

# Save to file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/qualifying_products_batch1.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(qualifying_products, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n‚úì Saved {len(qualifying_products)} products to qualifying_products_batch1.json")
 code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

import json

# Load the email template and subscriber data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/email_template.txt', 'r') as f:
    email_template = f.read()

with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/subscriber.json', 'r') as f:
    subscriber_data = json.load(f)

# Load qualifying products
qualifying_products = [
    {
        "id": 341,
        "name": "Charger v11",
        "date_created": "2025-02-09T23:07:26",
        "sales": 4,
        "regular_price": 49.99,
        "sale_price": 34.99,
        "discount_ratio": (49.99 - 34.99) / 49.99
    },
    {
        "id": 178,
        "name": "Old Sneakers 2022",
        "date_created": "2025-03-31T23:07:26",
        "sales": 5,
        "regular_price": 159.99,
        "sale_price": 72.99,
        "discount_ratio": (159.99 - 72.99) / 159.99
    }
]

# Sort by date (earliest first), then by discount ratio (smallest first)
qualifying_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['date_created'], x['discount_ratio']))

# Get top 3 products (we only have 2, so we'll use both)
top_products = qualifying_products[:3]

# Create email content for each subscriber
subscribers = subscriber_data['subscriber_list']

print(f"Preparing emails for {len(subscribers)} subscribers")
print(f"Using {len(top_products)} clearance products\n")

# Generate email content
email_contents = []

for subscriber in subscribers:
    email_body = email_template.replace('{customer_fullname}', subscriber['name'])
    
    # Build product list
    product_lines = []
    for i, product in enumerate(top_products, 1):
        line = f"{product['name']} - Original Price: ${product['regular_price']:.2f} - Promotional Price: ${product['sale_price']:.2f}"
        product_lines.append(line)
    
    # Replace placeholders in template
    # The template has 3 product placeholders, but we only have 2 products
    # Let's handle this gracefully
    
    if len(top_products) >= 1:
        email_body = email_body.replace('[Product Name 1]', top_products[0]['name'])
        email_body = email_body.replace('[Original Price]', f"${top_products[0]['regular_price']:.2f}", 1)
        email_body = email_body.replace('[Promotional Price]', f"${top_products[0]['sale_price']:.2f}", 1)
    
    if len(top_products) >= 2:
        # Find the second occurrence
        email_body = email_body.replace('[Product Name 2]', top_products[1]['name'])
        # For subsequent replacements, we need to be more careful
        parts = email_body.split('[Original Price]')
        if len(parts) > 2:
            parts[2] = parts[2].replace('[Original Price]', f"${top_products[1]['regular_price']:.2f}", 1)
            email_body = '[Original Price]'.join(parts[:2]) + parts[2]
        
        parts = email_body.split('[Promotional Price]')
        if len(parts) > 2:
            parts[2] = parts[2].replace('[Promotional Price]', f"${top_products[1]['sale_price']:.2f}", 1)
            email_body = '[Promotional Price]'.join(parts[:2]) + parts[2]
    
    # Remove the third product line if we don't have 3 products
    if len(top_products) < 3:
        # Remove the line with [Product Name 3]
        lines = email_body.split('\n')
        filtered_lines = [line for line in lines if '[Product Name 3]' not in line]
        email_body = '\n'.join(filtered_lines)
    
    email_contents.append({
        'to': subscriber['email'],
        'name': subscriber['name'],
        'subject': 'Special Clearance Promotion - Amazing Discounts!',
        'body': email_body
    })
    
    print(f"‚úì Email prepared for {subscriber['name']} ({subscriber['email']})")

# Save email contents for review
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/prepared_emails.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(email_contents, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n‚úì {len(email_contents)} emails prepared and saved")
print("\nEmail preview for first subscriber:")
print("="*80)
print(f"To: {email_contents[0]['to']}")
print(f"Subject: {email_contents[0]['subject']}")
print("\nBody (first 500 chars):")
print(email_contents[0]['body'][:500])
print("...")

fill="#FFF"/></g></svg> `woocommerce woo_products_update`

<Expandable title="Details">
```python

import json

# Load the email template and subscriber data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/email_template.txt', 'r') as f:
    email_template = f.read()

with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/subscriber.json', 'r') as f:
    subscriber_data = json.load(f)

# Qualifying products (sorted by date, then discount ratio)
qualifying_products = [
    {
        "id": 341,
        "name": "Charger v11",
        "date_created": "2025-02-09T23:07:26",
        "sales": 4,
        "regular_price": 49.99,
        "sale_price": 34.99,
        "discount_ratio": 0.3001
    },
    {
        "id": 178,
        "name": "Old Sneakers 2022",
        "date_created": "2025-03-31T23:07:26",
        "sales": 5,
        "regular_price": 159.99,
        "sale_price": 72.99,
        "discount_ratio": 0.5440
    }
]

# Get top 3 products (we have 2)
top_products = qualifying_products[:3]

# Create email content for each subscriber
subscribers = subscriber_data['subscriber_list']

email_contents = []

for subscriber in subscribers:
    # Start with template
    email_body = email_template.replace('{customer_fullname}', subscriber['name'])
    
    # Build product list manually
    product_list = ""
    for i, product in enumerate(top_products):
        product_list += f"{product['name']} - Original Price: ${product['regular_price']:.2f} - Promotional Price: ${product['sale_price']:.2f}\n"
    
    # Replace the product section in the template
    # Find and replace the product lines
    lines = email_body.split('\n')
    new_lines = []
    in_product_section = False
    product_section_start = -1
    
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        if 'üî• Featured Clearance Items:' in line:
            new_lines.append(line)
            new_lines.append('')
            # Add our products
            for product in top_products:
                new_lines.append(f"{product['name']} - Original Price: ${product['regular_price']:.2f} - Promotional Price: ${product['sale_price']:.2f}")
            in_product_section = True
        elif '[Product Name' in line and in_product_section:
            # Skip template product lines
            continue
        elif 'üìÖ Promotion Details:' in line:
            in_product_section = False
            new_lines.append('')
            new_lines.append(line)
        elif not in_product_section or '[Product Name' not in line:
            new_lines.append(line)
    
    email_body = '\n'.join(new_lines)
    
    email_contents.append({
        'to': subscriber['email'],
        'name': subscriber['name'],
        'subject': 'Special Clearance Promotion - Amazing Discounts!',
        'body': email_body
    })

# Save and display
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/final_emails.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(email_contents, f, indent=2)

print(f"‚úì Prepared {len(email_contents)} emails\n")
print("Email preview:")
print("="*80)
print(f"To: {email_contents[0]['to']}")
print(f"Subject: {email_contents[0]['subject']}")
print("\nBody:")
print(email_contents[0]['body'])
print("="*80)

print(f"\n‚úì Emails saved to final_emails.json")
print("\nReady to send emails!")
 code
```

import json
from datetime import datetime

# Create a comprehensive task completion report
report = {
    "task_completion_date": datetime.now().isoformat(),
    "summary": {
        "total_products_in_shop": 398,
        "products_filtered": 2,
        "products_moved_to_clearance": 2,
        "emails_sent": 3
    },
    "filter_criteria": {
        "in_stock_more_than_days": 90,
        "cutoff_date": "2025-07-19",
        "sales_less_than": 10
    },
    "category_created": {
        "id": 16,
        "name": "Outlet/Clearance",
        "slug": "outlet-clearance"
    },
    "qualifying_products": [
        {
            "id": 341,
            "name": "Charger v11",
            "date_created": "2025-02-09",
            "days_in_stock": 250,
            "sales_last_30_days": 4,
            "regular_price": 49.99,
            "sale_price": 34.99,
            "discount_percentage": 30.0
        },
        {
            "id": 178,
            "name": "Old Sneakers 2022",
            "date_created": "2025-03-31",
            "days_in_stock": 200,
            "sales_last_30_days": 5,
            "regular_price": 159.99,
            "sale_price": 72.99,
            "discount_percentage": 54.4
        }
    ],
    "emails_sent_to": [
        {"name": "John Zhang", "email": "jzhang@mcpt.com"},
        {"name": "Mike Li", "email": "mlie@mcpt.com"},
        {"name": "Tom Wang", "email": "tomw@mcpt.com"}
    ],
    "sorting_applied": {
        "primary": "stock-in time (earliest to latest)",
        "secondary": "discount ratio (smallest to largest)"
    }
}

# Save report
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/task_completion_report.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(report, f, indent=2)

# Print summary
print("="*80)
print("TASK COMPLETION REPORT")
print("="*80)
print(f"\nüìä Summary:")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Total products in shop: {report['summary']['total_products_in_shop']}")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Products meeting criteria: {report['summary']['products_filtered']}")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Products moved to Outlet/Clearance: {report['summary']['products_moved_to_clearance']}")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Emails sent to subscribers: {report['summary']['emails_sent']}")

print(f"\nüéØ Filter Criteria:")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ In stock for more than: {report['filter_criteria']['in_stock_more_than_days']} days")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Cutoff date: {report['filter_criteria']['cutoff_date']}")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Sales in last 30 days: < {report['filter_criteria']['sales_less_than']}")

print(f"\nüìÅ Category Created:")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ Name: {report['category_created']['name']}")
print(f"   ‚Ä¢ ID: {report['category_created']['id']}")

print(f"\nüì¶ Qualifying Products (sorted by date, then discount):")
for i, p in enumerate(report['qualifying_products'], 1):
    print(f"   {i}. {p['name']}")
    print(f"      - Created: {p['date_created']} ({p['days_in_stock']} days ago)")
    print(f"      - Sales (30 days): {p['sales_last_30_days']}")
    print(f"      - Price: ${p['sale_price']:.2f} (was ${p['regular_price']:.2f}) - {p['discount_percentage']:.1f}% off")

print(f"\nüìß Emails Sent To:")
for subscriber in report['emails_sent_to']:
    print(f"   ‚úì {subscriber['name']} ({subscriber['email']})")

print(f"\n‚úÖ Task completed successfully!")
print(f"   Report saved to: task_completion_report.json")
print("="*80)
